Bhandu bhowe bhatendaga labhanga lyamba, kwenda ku Liekalu kukwaapilikanishiya.
Shikukuu sha mikate jangatagwa ngedule, shishemwa pashaka, shatendaga bhandishila.
Ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila na bhaajiganya bha shalia, bhatendaga loleyanga mwa kwabhulajila a Yeshu, ikabhe bhatendaga kwaajogopanga bhandunji.
Bhai, Lishetani akwaajinjilaga a Yuda Ishikaliote, bhaliji munkumbi gwa mitume kumi na bhabhili bhala.
A Yuda gubhapite kunguluka na ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila na bhakulungwanji bha manjola, shibhapinga kwaendebhuka a Yeshu.
Nabhalabhonji guyaanonyelenje nigubhalegenenje kwaapa mmbiya.
A Yuda gubhakundile, gubhatemi nkuloleya malanga ga mmbone ga kwaatendebhuka a Yeshu gwangali kumumanya bhandu bhabhagwinji.
Bhai, lyubha lya mikate jangatagwa ngedule guliishile. Lyubhalyo lya ingwa mwana jwa ngondolo jwa pashaka.
Kwa nneyo a Yeshu gubhaatumilenje a Petili na a Yowana, gubhaalugulilenje, “Nnjendangane nkakolokoyanje shalya tulye pashaka.”
Gubhaabhushiyenje, “Punkupinga tukakolokoye kwei?”
Gubhaalugulilenje, “Mpilikananje! Pushinnjendangane kunnjini, shinng'imikananje na jwannume jumo ajigele lulo lwa mashi. Munkagulanje mpaka nnyumba jashaajinjile.
Mwaalugulilanje bhayene nyumba, ‘Bhaajiganya bhanakummuya, jili kwei kati jibhapinga lila pashaka na bhaajiganywa bhabho?’
Na bhenebho shibhannangulanje kati jikulungwa kugolopa jikonjeleywe, nnkolokoyanje mwenemo.”
Bhai, gubhapitengene, gubhaimenenje indu yowe malinga shibhabhalanjilwenje na a Yeshu, gubhakolokoyenje shalya sha pashaka.
Malanga gakatimilileje, a Yeshu gubhatemi pamo na mitume bhabho nkulya shalya.
Gubhaalugulilenje, “Njilokolila kaje kulya pashakaji pamo na mmanganya nganabhe potekwa.
Pabha ngajilya kabhili mpaka penepo pushijimalile mu Upalume gwa a Nnungu.”
Kungai gubhatolile shikombe sha divai, gubhatendile eja, gubhashite, “Ntolanje nnepesheyane mmowe.
Pabha ngunakummalanjilanga, ngang'wa kabhili divai ja shabhibhu mpaka Upalume gwa a Nnungu pushuishe.”
Kungai, gubhatolile nkate, gubhatendile eja, gubhaugebhenye, gubhaapelenje bhalinkuti, “Sheshino shiilu shangu shipinga shoywa kwa ligongo lyenunji. Ntendanje nnei kwa ngumbushila nne.”
Nneyo peyo bhakalyanganjeje gubhatolile shikombe, gubhashite, “Ashino shikombe shino, sha malagano ga ambi gakong'ondelwa na minyai jangu jijitika kwa ligongo lyenunji.
“Ikabheje, nnolanje! Andendebhuka jula pali na nne pamesha pepano.
Kweli Mwana juka Mundu anakwenda bhulagwa malinga shiipanjilwe, ikabheje ole, mundu andendebhuka.”
Penepo gubhatandubhenje kubhuyana ashaayene, gani shatende yeneyo.
Na kabhili nikoposhela mitau munkumbi gwabonji, kuti gani shabhe nkulungwa kupunda bhananji.
A Yeshu gubhaabhalanjilenje, “Bhapalume bha ilambo bhanakwaatagwalanga bhandu bhabhonji kwa mashili, ikabhe pubhaashemwanga ‘Bhamituka.’
Ikabheje mmanganya, inabhe nneyo, ali nkulungwa jwenunji anapinjikwa abhe nshoko jwa bhowe, na ali kalongolele abhe malinga ntumishi.
Igala jwei ali nkulungwa, atama kulya shalya, eu akolokoya jula? Penepo nkulungwa ni atama kulya! Ikabheje nne munkumbi gwetu muno, ni malinga ntumishi.”
“Mmanganya ntemingene na nne mobha ga lingwa kwangu,
na malinga atati shibhangamwiye upalume, nneyo peyo numbe nne ngunakunkamuyanga mmanganya.
Nkupinga nniyanganje na papila pamesha jangu, muupalume gwangu, na shintamangane mwiitengu ya ukulungwa kugaukumula makabhila kumi na gabhili ga Ishilaeli.”
A Yeshu gubhashite “A Shimoni, a Shimoni! Mpilikane! Lishetani anapinga ampembulanje mmanganya mbuti ngano.
Ikabheje nne ninnjujile mmwe a Shimoni, nkupinga ngulupai jenu jinapungushe. Na mmwe pushimmujilepo mwaataganje ntima ashaapwenu.”
Na a Petili gubhaajangwile, “Mmakulungwa, nne apano nili tayali kwenda tabhwa kumagelesha, nkali kuwa na mmwe.”
A Yeshu gubhaajangwile, “Ngunakummalanjila mmwe a Petili, lelo lipongo likanabhe kongobhela shinngane patatu.”
Kungai a Yeshu gubhaabhushiyenje bhaajiganywa bhabho, “Punantumilenje gwangali nng'uko gwa ela, wala nkobha gwa ilatu, mwatubhilwenje shoshowe?” Gubhajangwilenje, “Nng'oo twanngatubhilwa.”
Gubhaalugulilenje, “Ikabheje nnaino, jwene akwete nng'uko gwa ela jula ajigale, na akwete nkobha, nneyo peyo. Na jojowe jwangali upanga, aushe likoti lyakwe aume gumo.
Ngunakummalanjilanga, ganapinjikwa gatimilile majandiko gaanugula nne kuti, ‘Bhashinkubhikwa likundi limo na bhaalebhanga,’ elo, gowe gajandikwe kunugula nne ganapinjikwa gamalile.”
Na bhalabhonji gubhashitenje, “Mmakulungwa, nnole, apano jipali mipanga jibhili.” Na bhalabho gubhashite, “Bhai shijipwae.”
Na malinga shibhayobhelele, a Yeshu gubhapite kushitumbi sha Misheituni, bhaajiganywa bhabho gubhaakagwilenje.
Bhakaikanganeje kweneko gubhaalugulilenje, “Mwaajuganje a Nnungu nnajinjilanga mmalinjilo.”
Kungai gubhaaleshilenje bhaajiganywa bhabho, gubhapite kwa taliya kashoko kwa leshela mundu liganga kuika, gubhatindibhele nkwaajuga a Nnungu
bhalinkuti, “Atati, ibhaga nkupinga, nnjosheye shikombe sha mbotekoshi, nkali nneyo, itendeshe malinga shinkupinga mmwe, na wala nngabha malinga shingupinga nne.”
Malaika kukopoka kunnungu akwaakoposhelega kukwaataga ntima.
Bhali mmboteko ya kaje, gubhamindile kwaajuga a Nnungu, na matukuta gabho nibha mbuti mandondo ga minyai, galindolishila pai.
Bhakaajuganjeje a Nnungu, gubhabhujile kubhaajiganywa bhabho, gubhaaimenenje bhagonilenje lugono kwa totoshela nkuinjika.
Gubhaabhushiyenje, “Pakubha nnagonanga? Nnjumukanje maajuganje a Nnungu, nnajinjilanga mmalinjilo.”
A Yeshu bhakanabhe peya kubheleketa, likundi lya bhandunji guliishe lililongoywa na Yuda, bha munkumbi gwa kumi na bhabhili bhala. A Yuda gubhaabhandishile a Yeshu nkupinga kwaalamba.
Ikabheje a Yeshu gubhaabhalanjile, “A Yuda! Bhuli, nnakuntendebhuka Mwana juka Mundu kwa kunnamba?”
Bhaajiganywa bhabho bhakabhonanjeje nneila gubhashitenje, “Mmakulungwa, tutole mipanga jetu twaakapanje?”
Na jumo gwaleshele upanga mukantumishi jwa bhakulungwa bha bhaabhishila, gwankatile likutu lya kunnilo.
Penepo a Yeshu gubhashite, “Bhai nnekanje!” Gubhalikwashiye likutu lila, gubhannamiye.
Kungai a Yeshu gubhaabhalanjilenje ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila, na ashikalongolele bha bhalinda bha liekalu, na bhanangulungwa bhajilengene kukwakamula, “Bhuli, nnshikwiyangana kungamula na mipanga na ndonga mbuti nne nankupokonyola?
Mobha gowe gunaliji na mmanganya nniekalu nkangamulanga nkangamulangaga. Ikabheje gegano ni malanga genunji, malanga ga upalume gwa lubhindu.”
Bhai, gubhaakamulenje, gubhaatolilenje kwendanabhonji kwa akalongolele bha bhaabhishila. A Petili gubhakagwile nnyuma kwa kwaataliya.
Moto gwashinkukumbanywa pakati lugwani, gwaatemingene penepo pamo, na a Petili pubhaaliji popo.
Ntumishi jumo jwankongwe gwabhabhwene a Petili bhatemi tome pamoto, gwabhakolondolesheye meyo, nigwashite, “Abha bhandubha nnepeila pubhaliji na a Yeshu.”
Ikabheje a Petili gubhakanile bhalinkuti, “Gwee! Nne ngakwaamanya.”
Kashokope, mundu juna akwaabhonaga a Petili, nigwashite, “Numbe mmwe ni nkumbi gula.” Ikabheje a Petili gubhajangwile “Ika mmwe, nngabha nne!”
Ikapiteje malanga ga shaa jimo, mundu juna gwakomelesheye, “Kweli abha bhandubha pubhaliji na a Yeshu, pabha na bhalabho Bhagalilaya.”
Ikabheje a Petili gubhashite, “Ika mmwe, ngakwiimanya inkubheleketayo!” Na popo pepo, bhakanabhe maliya kubheleketa, lipongo gulikongobhele.
Bhakulungwa gubhatendebhwishe nikwaalola a Petili, na bhalabho a Petili gubhakumbushile gubhabhalanjilwe na Bhakulungwa, “Lipongo likanabhe kongobhela lelo, shinngane patatu.”
Penepo gubhakopweshe palanga gubhagutile kwa kaje.
Bhandunji bhaabhikaangaga a Yeshu muulinda, gubhaakomilenje na kwaalembula.
Gubhaatabhilenje shimbala kumeyo, nikwabhuyanga, “Nnondole! Ntulugulile gani ankomile.”
Gubhaabheleketelenje malobhe gamagwinji ga matukano.
Kukasheje, bhanangulungwa gubhaimenenje yani, ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila na bhaajiganya bha shalia. A Yeshu gubhapelekwe kulukumbilo.
Nigubhashitenje, “Ibhaga mmwe a Kilishitu ntubhalanjile?” A Yeshu gubhajangwile, “Nkali nimmalanjilangaga, nkakulupalilanga,
nkali nimmuyanje nkanyangulanga.
Ikabheje kutandubhila nnaino, Mwana juka Mundu shatame kunkono nnilo gwa Bhakulungwa a Nnungu Bhakwete Mashili.”
Penepo bhowenji nigubhashitenje “Igala tutende mmwe bhanabhabho a Nnungu?” Na bhalabho gubhashite, “Mmanganya ninkutinji Nne ni Jwenejo.”
Na bhalabhonji nigubhashitenje, “Bhuli, tupinga ukong'ondelo guna? Twaashayene tupilikene bhalibheleketa pa kang'wa jabho bhayene.”
Bhai likundi lyowe, gubhajimingene, nikwaapeleka a Yeshu kwa a Pilato.
Gubhatandubhenje kwaashitakiya bhalinkutinji, “Bhene bhandubha bhatendaga kwaapuganyanga bhandunji bhetu, bhalikwalimbiyanga kulipa koli kwa a Kaishali na bhalikwiishema a Kilishitu na a mpalume.”
A Pilato gubhaabhushiye a Yeshu, “Mmwe a mpalume bha Bhayaudi?” A Yeshu gubhaajangwile “Mmwe ni nkubheleketa.”
A Pilato gubhaabhalanjilenje ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila na lugwinjili lwa bhandu, “Ngakushibhona shibhalebhile abha bhandubha.”
Ikabheje na bhalabhonji gubhapundilenje kukwiya bhalinkutinji, “Bhanakwiya nnjasha kwa majiganyo gabho nshilambo showe sha ku Yudea, kundubhila ku Galilaya, mpaka apano.”
A Pilato bhakapilikaneje genego gubhabhushiye, “Bhuli, abha bhandubha bha ku Galilaya?”
Bhakamumanyeje kuti a Yeshu bhaliji mu Ukulungwa gwa a Elode, gubhaapeleshe kwa a Elode, pabha gene mobhago pubhaliji pa Yelushalemu pepala.
A Elode guyaanonyele bhakaabhoneje a Yeshu. Pabha bhapilikene ngani jabho, kwa nneyo kwa mobha gamagwinji bhatendaga loleya kwaabhona. Na kabhili bhatendaga pinga bhaabhone bhalitenda ilangulo.
Bhai, a Elode gubhakabhile nkwabhuya, ikabheje a Yeshu bhangaajangula shoshowe.
Ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila na bhaajandika bha shalia, gubhajimingene nkukong'ondela mashitaka gabhonji kwa kakati.
Bhai, a Elode na ashimanjola bhabho, gubhaalembulenje a Yeshu nikwatendela mbenji, kungai gubhaawashiyenje lijoo lya Upalume, gubhabhujilenabhonji kwa a Pilato.
A Elode na a Pilato bhukala pubhalinginji bhamagongo, kutandubhila lyene lyubhalyo gubhalinginji bhambwiga.
Bhai, a Pilato gubhashemile shitamo sha ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila na ashikalongolele bhana bha bhandunji,
gubhaabhalanjilenje, “Nshimbeleshelanga abha bhandubha kuti, bhanaapuganya bhandu. Ngakagulileje lyene lilobheli pameyo genunji, nangashibhona shibhalebhile shilingana na mashitaka genunji.
Numbe nngabha nne jikape, ikabhe nkali a Elode bhangashibhona shoshowe shibhalebhile, nigubhamujishiye. Pabha abha bhandubha shakwapi shibhatendile shapinjikwa bhaukumulwe kubhulagwa.
Kwa nneyo shinajile bhakomwe ibhoko, kungai shinaaleshelele.”
Pabha bhashinkupinjikwa kwaagopolelanga nkutabhwa jumo lyubha lya shikukuu.
Ikabheje bhowe gwaajobhelenje gwanakamo, “Mwaabhulaje abho, ntugopolele a Bhalabha!”
A Bhalabha bhashinkutabhwa kwa ligongo lya nnjasha yatendeshe pa shilambo na ligongo lya bhulaga bhandu.
A Pilato bhapinjile kwaaleshelela a Yeshu, bhai gubhakungulwishe kabhili na bhandunji,
ikabheje bhalabhonji gubhapundilenje jobhela, “Mwaakomele munshalabha, mwaakomele munshalabha!”
A Pilato gubhaabhalanjilenje gwatatu, “Bhalebhile nndi? Ngakushibhona shoshowe shibhalebhile shapinjikwa bhabhulagwe, kwa nneyo shindume bhakomwe ibhoko, naaleshelele.”
Ikabheje bhalabhonji gubhapundilenje kujobhela, kuti a Yeshu bhanapinjikwa bhakomelwe munshalabha. Kungai, malobhe gabhonji gugapilikanishe.
Bhai a Pilato gubhaukumwile kuti, itendeshe malinga shibhapinjilenje.
Gubhaaleshelele a Bhalabha bhatabhilwe kwa ligongo lya nnjasha na bhulaga bhandu. Gubhaakamwiye a Yeshu kwa ashimanjola, bhaatendelanje malinga shibhapingangaga.
Bhalinginji nkwaapeleka, gubhaimikenenje naka mundu jumo ashemwaga Shimoni jwa ku Kilene, alikopoka kunngunda. Bhai, gubhankamwilenje, gubhantwishilenje nshalabha gula aujigale nnyuma ja a Yeshu.
Bhandunji, makundi kwa makundi gubhaakagulenje, munkumbimo bhapalinji bhanabhakongwe bhaagutilangaga ililo.
A Yeshu gubhaatendebhushilenje, gubhashite, “Mmanganya ashinabhiti bha pa Yelushalemu! Nnang'utilanje nne, ikabhe mwiigutilanje mwaashayene na ashibhana bhenu.
Pabha, shigaishe mobha pushimmeleketanje, mbaya ashinannii na bhakanabhe kolanga wala kujonjeya!
Penepo, bhandunji shibhailugululanje itumbi, ‘Ntugwilanje!’ Na ijomboya, ‘Ntuunishilanje’!
Ibhaga bhandunji bhakuutendelanga nnei nkongo gwa mmii, shiibhe bhuli kwa nkongo gwa nnjumu?”
Bhandunji bhana bhabhili bhaalebhanga, bhashinkupelekwanga bhabhulagwanje pamo na a Yeshu.
Bhakaikanganeje pashemwaga, Shibhanga sha Ntwe, penepo gubhaakomelenje munshalabha a Yeshu na bhandunji bhabhili bhaalebhanga bhala, jumo kunkono nnilo, na juna kunkono nshinda.
A Yeshu gubhashite, “Atati mwaaleshelelanje, pabha bhakakwimanyanga ibhatendanga.” Gubhagebhenenje nngubho yabho kwa tendela shikoma.
Bhandunji gubhajimingene bhalilosheyanga. Na bhalabhonji ashikalongolele bha Shiyaudi gubhaatendelenje mbenji bhalinkutinji, “Bhashikwatapulanga bhananji, nnaino bhaitapule bhayene, monaga bhenebha bhali a Kilishitu bha a Nnungu!”
Ashimanjola nneyo peyo gubhaatendelenje mbenji a Yeshu, gubhaajendelenje nikwaapa divai ja shashama bhapapile,
bhalinkutinji, “Monaga mmwe nni A mpalume bha Bhayaudi, mwiitapule mmayene.”
Na pantundu nshalabha gwabho pashinkujandikwa mmbila “BHENEBHA A MPALUME BHA BHAYAUDI.”
Na nkulebha jumo akomelwe munshalabha jula, gwabhatukene alinkuti, “Bhuli, igala mmwe nngati a Kilishitu? Bhai mwiitapule mmayene, ntutapule na uwe.”
Ikabheje nkulebha juna jula gwankalipile mwine alinkuti, “Ugwe ukakwaajogopa a Nnungu? Numbe uli na ukumu jojo.
Uwe tushiukumulwa kwa aki, kwa itendi yetu. Ikabheje abha bhandubha shakwapi shoshowe shibhalebhile.”
Kungai nigwashite, “Mmwe a Yeshu! Nngumbushile pushinnjinjile mu Upalume gwenupo.”
A Yeshu gubhannjangwile, “Kweli ngunakuubhalanjila, lelope shuubhe na nne kupaladisho.”
Puyaaliji malanga ga shaa shita ja mui, lubhindu lukutabhaga shilambo showe mpaka shaa tisha,
na lukulungushi lwa Nniekalu lukupapukaga ipande ibhili.
A Yeshu gubhagutile kwa utiya, “Atati, mmakono genu ngunabhika mbumu yangu.” Bhakamaliyeje kubheleketa genego gubhamalile.
Penepo, bhakulungwa bha ashimanjola bhala bhakagabhoneje gatendeshe gala, gubhaaniye a Nnungu bhalinkuti, “Kweli abha bhandubha pubhaliji bha aki.”
Bhandu bhowe bhaikengene pepala kulolesheya genego, bhakagabhonanjeje gene gatendeshe gala, gubhabhujilengene kunngwabhonji, bhalikwikomanga pantima nkuinjika.
Ashambwiga ajabho a Yeshu, na bhanabhakongwe bhakagulangaga kukopoka ku Galilaya, gubhajimingene kwa talika bhalilolesheyanga genego.
Bhai bhashinkupagwa bhandu bhamo lina lyabho a Yoshepu, bhaliji bhanguja na bha aki. Pubhaliji bha lukumbi lukulu lwa Bhayaudi,
ikabheje bhenebho bhanganonyelwa na ukumu na itendi ya ashikalongolele ajabho. Bhenebha pubhaliji bhashilambo bha ku Alimataya shilambo sha Bhayaudi. Na bhatendaga lindilila kuika kwa Upalume gwa a Nnungu kwa nnolelo nkulu.
A Yoshepu gubhaajendele a Pilato, gubhajujile bhapegwe shiilu sha a Yeshu.
Kungai gubhatulwiye shiilu munshalabha, gubhailijilile shanda ja kitani ja mmbone, gubhabhishile nnikabhuli lyaolilwe nnindandawe likulungwa, lyaliji likanabhe shikwa mundu.
Pulyaaliji lyubha lya kolokoya indu ya Lyubha lya Pumulila, na pulyaaliji tome na tandubha.
Bhanabhakongwe bhajilengene pamo na a Yeshu kukopoka ku Galilaya, gubhaakagwilenje a Yoshepu, gubhaliweninji likabhuli na shibhashite kwaashika a Yeshu.
Kungai, gubhabhujengene kumui, gubhajenjilenje mauta ga nunjila ga kwenda pakaya shiilu sha a Yeshu. Lyubha lya Pumulila, gubhapumulilenje malinga shiyalajilwe na shalia.
Lyambape lyubha lya Jumapili, gubhapitengenenje kulikabhuli bhali bhajigelenje mauta ga nunjila gubhajenjilenje gala.
Gubhaimenenje liganga lya ibhila palikabhuli pala linokolelwe kunyenje likabhuli.
Bhakajinjilanjeje nkati, bhangashiimananga shiilu sha Bhakulungwa a Yeshu.
Bhalinginji nkukanganigwanga ga genego, shangupe bhandunji bhabhli bhawetenje nngubho ya ng'anyima mbuti kumeta kwa nnjai, bhajimingene pa tome.
Bhanabhakongwe bhala gubhajogopenje, gubhatindibhekelenje mpaka shenyi pantaka. Penepo bhandunji bhala gubhaalugulilenje, “Kwa nndi nkwaaloleyanga bhabhakoto munkumbi gwa bhawilenje?
Bhakwapi apano, bhayushile. Nkumbushilanje shibhammalanjilenje pubhaliji ku Galilaya kuti,
inapinjikwa Mwana juka Mundu akamuywe mmakono ga bhandunji bhakwetenje yambi, bhankomelanje munshalabha na lyubha lya tatu shayushe.”
Penepo bhanabhakongwe bhala, gubhakumbushilenje malobhe ga a Yeshu.
Bhakabhujanganeje kukopoka kumakabhuli, gubhapite kwaalugulilanga ashimitume kumi na jumo bhala, na bhananji gene gowego.
Bhene bhapelekenje jene nganijo kwa ashimitume pubhalinginji, a Malia Magidalena, a Yowana na a Malia anyinabhabho a Yakobho, na bhanabhakongwe bhana bhubhalongenabhonji.
Ikabheje bhapilikenenje bhala, bhangakulupalilanga pabha malobhe gala bhashinkubhoneka mbuti gangali mana.
Nkali nneyo, a Petili gubhajabhwile shibhutuka mpaka kulikabhuli. Bhakatepeje kuulumila nkati, gubhajibhwene shanda bhangashibhona shindu shina. Gubhaijabhulile akuno bhalipita kanganigwa ga yowe ikoposhele.
Lyubha lyolyo, bhandunji bhabhili munkumbi gwa bhaajiganywa bha a Yeshu, bhatendaga kwendangana kushijiji shimo shishemwa Emau, mwanja gwa maili shabha kukoposhela ku Yelushalemu.
Bhatendaga kungulushilanga gowe gakoposhele gala.
Bhalinginji nkukunguluka a Yeshu bhayene gubhakoposhele, gubhailundile.
Ikabheje meyo gabhonji gashinkugubhikwa bhanaamanyanje.
Gubhaabhushiyenje, “Nkukungulushilanga nndi akuno nnikwendangana?” Gubhajimingene akuno bhainjikenje kumeyo.
Jumo ashemwa Kileopashi gwabhajangwile, “Bhuli, pa Yelushalemu mmwe jikape mmajeni nkagugamanya gakoposhele kweneko agano mobha gano?”
Na bhalabho gubhabhushiye, “Gei genego?” Bhalabhonji gubhaajangulenje, “Ngani ja a Yeshu Bhanashaleti. Bhenebho pubhaliji ankulondola, bhakwete mashili gamakulungwa, kwa malobhe gabho na itendi yabho pa meyo ga a Nnungu na pabhandu bhowe.
Ashikalongolele bha bhaabhishila na ashikalongolele bhetu bhashinkwaakamulanga nikwaukumula bhabhulagwe, gubhaakomelelenje munshalabha
Ikabheje twakulupalile kuti bhenebho shibhajigombole Ishilaeli. Kupunda gene gowego, lelo lyubha lya tatu tandubhila pugatendeshe.
Na kabhili bhanabhakongwe bhana bha munkumbi gwetu bhashikutuimuyanga. Bhashinkwendangana kulikabhuli lyambape,
bhangashiimananga shiilu shabho. Gubhabhujengene gubhashitenje kuti bhashinkukoposhelwanga na ashimalaika bha kunnungu bhalugulenje kuti a Yeshu bhabhakoto.
A Shaajetunji bhapitengene kulikabhuli gubhakong'ondelenje ibhalugulenje bhanabhakongwe ila, ikabheje bhangaabhonanga.”
Kungai a Yeshu gubhaalugulilenje, “Pakubha mmanganya mmangumba nneyo na mitima jenunji jinatopa kukulupalila gowe galugwilwe na ashinkulondola bha a Nnungu!
Bhuli, a Kilishitu bhakapinjikweje kupotekwa, na kwa nneyo bhajinjile muukonjelo gwabho?”
Gubhaatalashiyenje gowe gaatayaga bhenebho, Mmajandiko kutandubhila a Musha mpaka ashinkulondola bhowe bha a Nnungu.
Bhakabhandishilanjeje shijiji shibhajendanganaga shila, a Yeshu gubhatendile mbuti bhanapunda kwenda mmujo.
Ikabheje bhanganya bhala gubhaashondelesheyenje bhalinkutinji, “Ntame pano na uwe, pabha kunapilila, na shilo shinabhandishila.” Bhai, gubhajinjile nnyumba, gubhateminabhonji.
Bhakatameje kulya nabhonji, gubhatolile nkate, gubhatendile eja kwa a Nnungu, gubhaugebhenye, gubhaapelenje.
Shangu meyo gabhonji gakutandanukaga, gubhaamanyinji, ikabheje bhenebho gubhaobhile pa meyo gabhonji.
Bhai, gubhabhalanjilenenje, “Bhuli mitima jetu jikakolelaga nkwiinonyela, pubhatutalashiyaga Majandiko mumpanda mula?”
Gubhajabhulengenenje gene malanga pegala, gubhabhujengene ku Yelushalemu. Gubhaaimenenje bhaajiganywa kumi na jumo bhala, na bhandunji bhatemingene pamo
bhalibheleketanga, “Kweli bhakulungwa bhayushile, bhaakoposhele a Shimoni.”
Bhai, bhene bhaajiganywa bhabhili bhala gubhaalugulilenje gowe gaaimenenje mumpanda, na shibhashite kwaamanyanga a Yeshu nkugabhanya nkate.
Bhalinginji nkutalashiya genego a Yeshu bhayene gubhajimi pakati jabhonji, gubhaabhalanjilenje, “Ulele ubhe na mmanganya.”
Gubhaimukenje na jogopa kujila bhakulibhonanga lioka.
Ikabheje a Yeshu gubhaabhalanjilenje, “Kwa nndi nnajogopanga? Kwa nndi nnakolanga lipamba mmitima jenunji?
Nnolanje makono na makongono gangu, kuti ni nne namwene. Mmbapayanje mmonanje, pabha lioka lyangali shiilu na maupa malinga shinkumonanga shino.”
Bhakabheleketeje genego, Gubhaalangulenje makono na makongono gabho.
Bhangakulupalilanga kwa ligongo lya kwiinonyela na kanganigwa, a Yeshu gubhaabhushiyenje, “Pepano nkwetenje shalya shoshowe?”
Gubhaapelenje shipande sha shamaki jwa joka.
Gubhatolile, nigubhatawine bhowe bhalikwaalolanga.
Kungai gubhaalugulilenje, “Gegano ni gunamalanjilenje punaliji pamo na mmanganya, kuti gowe gajandikwe ga nugula nne, Nshalia ja a Musha, na Ashinkulondola, na Shabhuli ganapinjikwa gatimilile.”
Penepo, gubhaapelenje lunda lwa kugamanya Majandiko.
Gubhaalugulilenje, “Ishijandikwa, kuti a Kilishitu shibhapotekwe na lyubha lya tatu shibhayushe.
Na kuti, kwiipeta na kuleshelelwa kwa yambi shikulunguywe kupitila lina lyabho, kuumila ku Yelushalemu.
Mmanganya ni mmaakong'ondela bha genega.
Nnolanje, shinimpeleshelanje miadi ja Atati, ikabheje ntamangane pano, mpaka pushinimpeleshelanje mashili ga kopoka kunnungu.”
Kungai gubhalongoyenje mpaka ku Bhetania, gubhajinwile makono gabho kunani, nigubhaajujilenje mboka.
Akuno bhalikwaajujilanga mboka, gubhaaleshilenje, gubhatolilwe kunani kunnungu.
Gubhaatindibhalilenje, nigubhabhujilengene ku Yelushalemu bhalikwinonyelanga kwa kaje.
Gubhatemingenenje mobha gowe Nniekalu bhalikwainiyanga a Nnungu.
